*ašk-a:čyemwi-wa F aška:čimowa, he newly talks

*na:t-a:čyemwi-wa M na:ta:čemow, he takes a message to the place
*po:n-a:čyemwi-wa M po:na:čemow, he stops narrating
*taθ-a:čyemwi-wa F tana:čimo:wa, he tells there
*awat-a:čyemwi-wa M awa:ta:čemow, he carries off a message

*axkw-a:čyemwi-mikatwi F ahkwa:čimo:mikatwi, it narrates so far

483. *yeθkwe:w woman (alternate form of eθkwe:w)

484. *yi:wak, *yiwe: meat, flesh, muscle254
*ašk-yi:wak-a:ni M aski:wakan, raw meat, fresh meat
*ašk-yi:wak-ehkawi-wi M aski:wakɛ:hkaw, it moves as raw flesh
*aya:šk-yi:wak-ehkawi-wi M aya:skiwakɛ:hkaw, it moves as raw flesh
*kexpak-yi:wak-atwi M kɛhpa:ki:wakat, a thick cut of meat
*ašk-yi:waki-pwi-wa C aski:wakipo:w, he eats raw meat
*axpi:hč-yi:we:-ta:-makat-wi M ahpi:hčiwɛ:tamakat, it acts with that degree of strength
*axpi:hč-yi:we:-ta:-wa M ahpi:hčiwɛ:taw, he acts with that degree of strength
*axpi:hč-yi:we:-wa M ahpi:hčiwɛw, he has so much muscular strength
